      <div style="border:1px #FFFFFF solid; overflow:auto;"> 
       <h2 style="display: block; margin: 0; border: 0; padding: .4em .5em .2em; background-color: #d1e4ff; font-weight: bold; text-align: center;"><span id="Welcome_to_the_Community_portal.21"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Welcome_to_the_Community_portal!"> Welcome to the Community portal! </span></h2> 
       <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1007196855">.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutboxplain{float:right;margin:0 0 0 1em;border:1px solid #aaa;background:#fff;padding:0.3em 0.6em 0.2em 0.6em;text-align:center;font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutboxleft{float:left;margin:0 1em 0 0}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutlist{display:inline-block;border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;margin-bottom:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutboxplain>ul{font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutanchordiv{position:relative;top:-3em}.mw-parser-output li .module-shortcutanchordiv{float:right}.mw-parser-output .mbox-imageright .module-shortcutboxplain{padding:0.4em 1em 0.4em 1em;line-height:1.3}</style>
       <div class="module-shortcutanchordiv">
        <span id="P:WP"></span><span id="WP:COM"></span>
       </div>
       <div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note">
        <div class="module-shortcutlist">
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcuts</a>
        </div>
        <ul>
         <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=P:WP&amp;redirect=no">P:WP</a></span></li>
         <li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:COM&amp;redirect=no">WP:COM</a></span></li>
        </ul>
       </div> 
       <p>This page provides a listing of current collaborations, tasks, and news about English Wikipedia. New to Wikipedia? See the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Contributing_to_Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia:Contributing to Wikipedia">contributing to Wikipedia</a> page or <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction" title="Help:Introduction">our tutorial</a> for everything you need to know to get started. For a listing of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ADMINP" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ADMINP">internal project pages</a> of interest, see the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Department_directory" title="Wikipedia:Department directory">department directory</a>. </p> 
      </div> 
      <div style="margin-top:2em; border:1px #FFFFFF solid; text-align:center;">

      <div style="margin-top:2em; border:1px #FFFFFF solid;"> 
       <h2 style="display: block; margin: 0; border: 0; padding: .4em .5em .2em; background-color: #d1e4ff; font-weight: bold; text-align: center;"><span class="mw-headline" id="Help_out"> Help out </span></h2> 
       <p><br> </p> 
       <p style="margin: .8em 0;"> You can help improve the articles listed below! This list updates frequently, so check back here for more tasks to try. (See <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Task_Center" title="Wikipedia:Task Center">Wikipedia:Task Center</a></b> for brief guides.) </p> 
       <div style="display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; overflow: auto;"> 
        <div role="region" aria-labelledby="copyedit-label" style="float: left; box-sizing: border-box; width: 33.33%; padding: 0.1em;"> 
         <div id="copyedit-label" style="text-align:center; background: #f7f7f7; border: 1px solid #aaaaaa; padding: .4em; font-size: 110%; font-weight: bold;">
          Fix spelling and grammar 
         </div> 
         <div id="copyedit"> 
          <ul>
           <li><a href="/wiki/El_Zapotal" title="El Zapotal">El Zapotal</a></li>

       <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="General_notices">General notices</span></h3> 
       <ul id="watchlist-message" style="margin-bottom:0.5em"> 
        <li class="watchlist-message cookie-ID_484">Two <span style="font-weight: bold;"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_adminship" title="Wikipedia:Requests for adminship">requests for adminship</a></span> are open for discussion.</li> 
       </ul> 
       <ul>
        <li>Do you have need for a specialized script that doesn't exist yet, or have an idea for a cool new script or gadget? Post requests and ideas at <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:User_scripts/Requests" title="Wikipedia:User scripts/Requests">Wikipedia:User scripts/Requests</a></b>.</li>
       </ul> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Projects_seeking_help">Projects seeking help</span></h4> 
       <p><i>Also consider posting WikiProject, Task Force, and Collaboration news at the Signpost's <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Wikipedia_Signpost/Newsroom/WikiProject_desk#Sidebar_news_requests" title="Wikipedia:Wikipedia Signpost/Newsroom/WikiProject desk">WikiProject Report</a> page.</i> </p> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="WikiProjects_and_Task_Forces"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject">WikiProjects</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Council/Guide/Task_forces" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Council/Guide/Task forces">Task Forces</a></span></h4> 
       <ul>
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Sweep" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Sweep">WikiProject Sweep</a></b>, which aims to comprehensively review every article created in Wikipedia's early days to ensure basic conformity to modern standards, has been launched following a successful <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Council/Proposals/Sweep" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Council/Proposals/Sweep">proposal at the WikiProject Council</a>.</li> 
        <li>The <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Help_Project" title="Wikipedia:Help Project">Wikipedia Help Project</a></b> seeks assistance expanding and improving the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Task_Center" title="Wikipedia:Task Center">Task Center</a> and other pages within the <a href="/wiki/Help:Contents" title="Help:Contents">Help namespace</a>.</li> 
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Abandoned_Drafts/Stale_drafts" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Abandoned Drafts/Stale drafts">WikiProject Abandoned Drafts Stale draft drive</a>.</b> An ongoing drive dedicated to reducing the amount of stale user space drafts. Options are to delete, redirect, move to mainspace or blank. Stop by and help the drive out!</li> 
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Spoken_Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Spoken Wikipedia">WikiProject Spoken Wikipedia</a></b> is looking for people who are interested in helping out in our project to get our articles into an audio format that can be used for any number of uses including, but not limited to, visually impaired or people who just prefer to listen to the article instead of reading it for whatever reason they choose. You can sign up here on <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Spoken_Wikipedia/Participants" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Spoken Wikipedia/Participants">our participant's page</a>. <b>We are also in need of native or fluent speakers</b> so that everything is pronounced properly. You can sign up for the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Spoken_Wikipedia/Pronunciation_task_force" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Spoken Wikipedia/Pronunciation task force">Pronunciation task force</a> by adding your name as well as your languages of fluency to section 2.</li>
       </ul> 
       <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Technical_news">Technical news</span></h3> 
       <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable relarticle mainarticle selfreference noprint">
        This section is <a href="/wiki/Help:Transclusion" title="Help:Transclusion">transcluded</a> from <a href="/wiki/Template:Latest_tech_news" title="Template:Latest tech news">Template:Latest tech news</a>. <span class="plainlinks" style="font-style: normal"><span style="font-size:85%;">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Latest_tech_news&amp;action=edit">edit</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Latest_tech_news&amp;action=history">history</a>)</span></span>
       </div> 
       <p><br> </p> 
       <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_efforts_and_monthly_projects">Group efforts and monthly projects</span></h3> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monthly_projects">Monthly projects</span></h4> 
       <ul>
        <li><b>Guild of Copy Editors' editing drive.</b> The <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Guild_of_Copy_Editors/Backlog_elimination_drives/May_2021" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Guild of Copy Editors/Backlog elimination drives/May 2021">May 2021 backlog drive</a> is a one-month-long effort of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Guild_of_Copy_Editors" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Guild of Copy Editors"><b>Guild of Copy Editors</b></a> to reduce the backlog of articles that require copy editing; those carrying the {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy_edit" title="Template:Copy edit">copy edit</a>}} tag (also {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Awkward" title="Template:Awkward">awkward</a>}}, {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy_edit_section" title="Template:Copy edit section">copy edit section</a>}}, {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Inappropriate_person" title="Template:Inappropriate person">inappropriate person</a>}}, and {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Copy_edit_inline" title="Template:Copy edit inline">copy edit inline</a>}} and their redirects) or listed on the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GOCE/REQ" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:GOCE/REQ">GOCE Requests page</a>. <u>It ended on 31 May 2021, 23:59 (UTC). Stay tuned for the next event.</u></li>
       </ul> 
       <p><br> </p> 
       <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ongoing_group_efforts">Ongoing group efforts</span></h4> 
       <ul>
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:The_100,000_Challenge" title="Wikipedia:The 100,000 Challenge">The 100,000 Challenge</a>.</b> The quest to bring about 100,000 article improvements and creations globally through a series of 50,000/10,000/1000 Challenges for different regions and countries. This is a loose challenge, a list will not be maintained here, but the components will function independently on each of the subpages. Will be updated every week or two. 
         <ul>
          <li><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:The_50,000_Destubbing_Challenge" title="Wikipedia:The 50,000 Destubbing Challenge">The 50,000 Destubbing Challenge</a> is a long term challenge to destub 50,000 articles on English Wikipedia for every country and topic. It may take decades to accomplish, it may take ten years, it all depends on how many people actively contribute.</li>
         </ul></li>
       </ul> 
       <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
        Page used for announcements towards the community members of the project
       </div> 
       <ul>
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiCup" title="Wikipedia:WikiCup">Wikipedia:WikiCup</a></b>. The WikiCup is a championship that has taken place every year on Wikipedia since 2007. The Cup is played and won by skill of editing. The purpose of the Cup is to encourage content creation and improvement and make editing on Wikipedia more fun. There is a new round every month, until the current contest ends; below are the details. 
         <ul>
          <li>May 1 to June 28 – 32 contestants left.</li> 
          <li>July 1 to August 29 – 16 contestants left.</li> 
          <li>September 1 to October 31 – 8 finalists left, the contestant with the highest score will win!</li>
         </ul></li> 
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:The_Core_Contest" title="Wikipedia:The Core Contest">WP:The Core Contest</a></b> is a recurring six-week contest, starting on June 1 in 2021. The purpose is to give a boost to Wikipedia's most important articles, especially those that start out in a bad shape.</li> 
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Military_history/Contest" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Military history/Contest">Monthly contest, WikiProject Military history</a>.</b> The contest department of the Military history WikiProject aims to motivate increased quality in military history articles by offering a form of friendly competition for project members making improvements to them. The primary contest available is a simple rolling competition that awards points for improving articles. The contest runs from the first to last day of each month.</li> 
        <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Medicine/Collaboration_of_the_Month" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Medicine/Collaboration of the Month">WikiProject Medicine Collaboration of the Month</a>.</b> Every month, a topic will be selected from this page that will be the focus of editing for some members of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Medicine" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Medicine">Wikipedia:WikiProject Medicine</a>. The article may or may not yet exist. Topics may either relate to medical basic sciences (anatomy, biochemistry, and so on), or clinical medicine (illnesses, surgical procedures, and so on).</li>
       </ul>

        </caption>

       <h2 style="display: block; margin: 0 0 .75em; border: 0; padding: .4em .5em .2em; background-color: #d1e4ff; font-weight: bold;"><span class="mw-headline" id="Tip_of_the_day"> Tip of the day </span></h2> 
       <div role="complementary" aria-labelledby="totd-label" style="overflow:hidden; box-sizing:border-box; margin:0.5em auto 0; border:solid medium #ADD8E6; border-radius:15px; width:90%; padding:1.4em 0.9em 1em 1.2em;"> 
        <div id="totd-label" style="font-size:90%;">
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Tip_of_the_day" title="Wikipedia:Tip of the day">Tip of the day...</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="floatright">
         <img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png/120px-Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png" decoding="async" width="120" height="125" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png/180px-Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png/240px-Simple_light_bulb_graphic.png 2x" data-file-width="717" data-file-height="744">

         <span style="font-size: 120%;"><b>Look before you leap</b></span>
        </div> 
        <p>Before you <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Your_first_article" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Your first article">write a new article</a> from scratch, please do a <a href="/wiki/Help:Searching" title="Help:Searching">search</a> to make sure you are not creating a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Duplicate_articles" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Duplicate articles">duplicate</a> of an article that already exists.
